The phrase Sometimes a cigar is just a cigar is a famous quote by the American philosopher and writer, Mark Twain. The phrase is often used to mean that something is what it appears to be, and nothing more. It is a way of saying that there is no hidden meaning or deeper significance to something, and that it should be taken at face value.
